# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

propagators. This is the recommended propagator set.\\n\\n**HTTP Server-Side (Incoming):** In `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/filters/traces.go`, the `WithTracing()` function (line 34) wraps HTTP handlers using `otelhttp.NewHandler()` with propagators configured via `otelhttp.WithPropagators(tracing.Propagators())` (line 36). The otelhttp library automatically extracts trace context from incoming request headers.\\n\\n**HTTP Client-Side (Outgoing):** The `WrapperFor()` function (line 119) in utils.go returns a transport wrapper that uses `otelhttp.NewTransport()` (line 127) with the same propagators, enabling automatic trace context injection into outgoing HTTP requests.\\n\\n### Grafana (grafana/grafana)\\n\\n**Core Infrastructure:** `pkg/infra/tracing/tracing.go` implements the central tracing service with support for both W3C and Jaeger propagators. The `Inject()` method (line 345) injects trace context into HTTP headers using `otel.GetTextMapPropagator().Inject(ctx, propagation.HeaderCarrier(header))`.\\n\\n**HTTP Server-Side (Incoming - Request Tracing):** `pkg/middleware/request_tracing.go` implements the `RequestTracing()` middleware (line 94) which extracts trace context from incoming requests at line 103 using `otel.GetTextMapPropagator().Extract(req.Context(), propagation.HeaderCarrier(req.Header))`. In the `Run()` method (line 61), it sets the global TextMapPropagator: `otel.SetTextMapPropagator(propagation.TraceContext{})` (line 62). This uses the standard W3C Trace Context format.\\n\\n**HTTP Client-Side (Outgoing):** `storage/remote/client.go` - Both `NewReadClient()` (line 151) and `NewWriteClient()` (line 183) use `otelhttp.NewTransport()` to wrap the HTTP client transport. For write clients, this is explicitly shown at lines 223-227 where `otelhttp.NewTransport()` is called with HTTP trace options, enabling automatic trace context injection into remote write requests.\\n\\n### Pattern Summary\\n\\nAll three services follow the same OpenTelemetry propagation pattern:\\n1. **Configuration:** Set global TextMapPropagator using `otel.SetTextMapPropagator()` with composite propagators\\n2. **Server-side (Extract):** Use `TextMapPropagator.Extract(ctx, carrier)` to extract from request headers (`propagation.HeaderCarrier`)\\n3. **Client-side (Inject):** Use `TextMapPropagator.Inject(ctx, carrier)` to inject into outgoing request headers\\n4. **Instrumentation:** Use otelhttp/otelgrpc libraries that handle propagation automatically\\n\\nThe implementation supports fallback mechanisms (e.g., Grafana's custom header handling) and can compose multiple propagator formats (W3C Trace Context + Baggage + Jaeger) to ensure compatibility across different tracing backends.\"\n}\n",

This uses the standard W3C Trace Context format.\\n\\n**HTTP Client-Side (Outgoing):** `storage/remote/client.go` - Both `NewReadClient()` (line 151) and `NewWriteClient()` (line 183) use `otelhttp.NewTransport()` to wrap the HTTP client transport. For write clients, this is explicitly shown at lines 223-227 where `otelhttp.NewTransport()` is called with HTTP trace options, enabling automatic trace context injection into remote write requests.\\n\\n### Pattern Summary\\n\\nAll three services follow the same OpenTelemetry propagation pattern:\\n1. **Configuration:** Set global TextMapPropagator using `otel.SetTextMapPropagator()` with composite propagators\\n2. **Server-side (Extract):** Use `TextMapPropagator.Extract(ctx, carrier)` to extract from request headers (`propagation.HeaderCarrier`)\\n3. **Client-side (Inject):** Use `TextMapPropagator.Inject(ctx, carrier)` to inject into outgoing request headers\\n4. **Instrumentation:** Use otelhttp/otelgrpc libraries that handle propagation automatically\\n\\nThe implementation supports fallback mechanisms (e.g., Grafana's custom header handling) and can compose multiple propagator formats (W3C Trace Context + Baggage + Jaeger) to ensure compatibility across different tracing backends.\"\n}\n",
